				</div><p><img class="alignnone wp-image-8544 size-full" src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/plugins/speed-booster-pack/inc/images/1x1.trans.gif" data-lazy-src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Shots-600.jpg" alt="Calgary Region restaurants - food shots" width="600" height="263" srcset="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Shots-600-300x132.jpg 300w, http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Shots-600-325x142.jpg 325w, http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Shots-600.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px" /><noscript><img class="alignnone wp-image-8544 size-full" src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Shots-600.jpg" alt="Calgary Region restaurants - food shots" width="600" height="263" srcset="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Shots-600-300x132.jpg 300w, http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Shots-600-325x142.jpg 325w, http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Shots-600.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px" /></noscript></p>
<p><strong>By Chad Hason</strong><strong>, Content Contributor</strong></p>
<p>I travel a lot, and often relied on the kindness of people who appear both local and well-fed to steer me to the best places to eat.</p>
<p>It’s not enough to be delicious &#8211; I also appreciate a good deal.</p>
<p>Why should my home town and surrounding region be any different?</p>
<p>Without further adieu &#8211; here are my <strong>top five recommendations for anyone who wants to eat deliciously inexpensive local treats</strong>!</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h2><strong>1. <a href="http://lavidaloca.ca/Home/tabid/114365/Default.aspx" target="_blank">La Vida Loca</a></strong></h2>
<p><img class="size-full wp-image-8541 alignnone" src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/plugins/speed-booster-pack/inc/images/1x1.trans.gif" data-lazy-src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Mexican-600.jpg" alt="Calgary Region restaurants - mexican" width="600" height="263" srcset="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Mexican-600-300x132.jpg 300w, http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Mexican-600-325x142.jpg 325w, http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Mexican-600.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px" /><noscript><img class="size-full wp-image-8541 alignnone" src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Mexican-600.jpg" alt="Calgary Region restaurants - mexican" width="600" height="263" srcset="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Mexican-600-300x132.jpg 300w, http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Mexican-600-325x142.jpg 325w, http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Mexican-600.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px" /></noscript></p>
<p>Located downtown Calgary on sunny 17th AVE SW, La Vida Loca offers authentic Mexican cuisine &#8211; we’re talking about momma’s recipes passed down to her son.</p>
<p>An owner who passes her passion for the art of Mexican food along to those who appreciate little touches and big flavour.</p>
<p>Fresh guacamole is made right in front of you.</p>
<p>The tortillas are warm, soft and homemade and the masterful presentation of each unique plate is the only reason to hold yourself back from devouring each item &#8211; if only for a brief, spectacular moment.</p>
<p>All for a price that makes it hard to understand whether this is chic dining or good ol’ street food.</p>
<p>Mondays and Wednesdays are taco night &#8211; where you get the same amazing tacos (your choice of fillings) at a discounted price. Perfect for first-time tasters.</p>
<p>Speaking of perfect &#8211; I recommend enjoying them with a freshly blended margarita on their oversized patio surrounded by palm trees and classic lanterns&#8230;once the weather warms up, of course.</p>
<p>Between its patio, price and portions &#8211; you’d be hard-pressed to find better Mexican cuisine this side of Mexico.</p>

<div class='tm-ctt-tip'></div>
</div>
<p><strong><u>Top Five Dishes</u></strong><br />
<u></u></p>
<p><strong>Personal Favourite:</strong><br />
Fish Tacos</p>
<p><strong>Authentic Dish:</strong><br />
Chicken Mole Classic Tacos (with guac, of course)</p>
<p><strong>Veggie Lover: </strong><br />
Ceviche (take your pick- they are all amazing)</p>
<p><strong>Sweet Tooth:</strong><br />
Fresh Churros!</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h2><strong>2. <a href="http://wopizza.ca/" target="_blank">Without Papers </a></strong></h2>
<p><img class="alignright wp-image-8542 size-large" src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/plugins/speed-booster-pack/inc/images/1x1.trans.gif" data-lazy-src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Pizza1-600-360x480.jpg" alt="Calgary Region restaurants-pizza " width="360" height="480" srcset="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Pizza1-600-225x300.jpg 225w, http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Pizza1-600-360x480.jpg 360w, http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Pizza1-600-325x433.jpg 325w, http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Pizza1-600.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 360px) 100vw, 360px" /><noscript><img class="alignright wp-image-8542 size-large" src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Pizza1-600-360x480.jpg" alt="Calgary Region restaurants-pizza " width="360" height="480" srcset="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Pizza1-600-225x300.jpg 225w, http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Pizza1-600-360x480.jpg 360w, http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Pizza1-600-325x433.jpg 325w, http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Pizza1-600.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 360px) 100vw, 360px" /></noscript>I try to keep an open mind when it comes to some things &#8211; but when it comes to the best darn thin-crust pizza in Calgary &#8211; you’d be hard-pressed to beat Without Papers.</p>
<p>Now to be fair &#8211; I love a lot of pizza places in Calgary &#8211; and I agree that different strokes appeal to different folks.</p>
<p>But when my friend Jordan originally gave me a bite of the cold Without Papers Pizza leftovers he forgot in his car &#8211; even that, at the time, was the best pizza I’ve ever had.</p>
<p>Their authentic, thin-crust style makes the only type of pizza that has me looking forward to getting to the crust – in fact, I personally roll each slice up so that I get a taste of the crust in every bite.</p>
<div class='tm-tweet-clear'></div>
<div class='tm-click-to-tweet'>
<div class='tm-ctt-text'><a href='https://twitter.com/share?text=I+personally+roll+each+slice+up+so+that+I+get+a+taste+of+the+crust+in+every+bite.&#038;via=calgaryregion&#038;related=calgaryregion&#038;url=http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/2016/02/10/5-hidden-culinary-treasures-calgary-region-inexpensive/' target='_blank'>I personally roll each slice up so that I get a taste of the crust in every bite.</a></div>
<p><a href='https://twitter.com/share?text=I+personally+roll+each+slice+up+so+that+I+get+a+taste+of+the+crust+in+every+bite.&#038;via=calgaryregion&#038;related=calgaryregion&#038;url=http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/2016/02/10/5-hidden-culinary-treasures-calgary-region-inexpensive/' target='_blank' class='tm-ctt-btn'>Click To Tweet</a>
<div class='tm-ctt-tip'></div>
</div>
<p>They are perfect for takeout on the way out of downtown, and in the spring, they deliver their pizza on old-school cruiser bikes &#8211; if you live close enough.</p>
<p>But the true experience involves going up the stairs to their sit-down restaurant.</p>
<p>Featuring a mix of comfortable booths and tables, the food is complemented by the showing of classic retro movies projected on the walls next to their colourful wall-mounted “movie-esque” posters, creatively promoting a wide variety of their patented pizza options.</p>
<p>And if you have problems sticking stuff to your fridge &#8211; good news, they let you take their fridge magnets home.</p>
<p><strong><u>Top Five Dishes</u></strong><br />
<u></u></p>
<p><strong>Personal Favourite: </strong><br />
The Hutch Pizza</p>
<p><strong>Authentic Dish:</strong><br />
Parma Pizza</p>
<p><strong>Veggie Lover:</strong><br />
Shroom Pizza</p>
<p><strong>Sweet Tooth: </strong><br />
Sweet Julie Dessert Pizza</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h2><strong>3. <a href="http://tuktukthai.com/" target="_blank">Tuk Tuk Thai</a></strong></h2>
<p><img class="alignright size-full wp-image-8540" src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/plugins/speed-booster-pack/inc/images/1x1.trans.gif" data-lazy-src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/logo-tuk-tuk-thai_150.jpg" alt="Calgary Region restaurants - tuk tuk thai" width="150" height="150" /><noscript><img class="alignright size-full wp-image-8540" src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/logo-tuk-tuk-thai_150.jpg" alt="Calgary Region restaurants - tuk tuk thai" width="150" height="150" /></noscript></p>
<p>Fast and flavourful. That’s their slogan &#8211; and if you know anything about the history of this newly opened 17th Ave Thai take-out &#8211; you can be sure it lives up to its name.</p>
<p>First of all &#8211; if you have lived in Calgary for any length of time, and have sought out the best Thai restaurants, I have no doubt you’ve already come across Thai Sa-on Royal Thai Cuisine.</p>
<p>Located on 10th AVE, this sit-down restaurant has been rated the best Thai food restaurant by the likes of John Gilchrist, Where Calgary, Fast Forward and even by Jackie Chan.</p>
<p>Known for delicious, authentic Thai, the ownership group decided to take their offering to the busy streets of Calgary.</p>
<p>They opened a small take-out restaurant that offers some of their most popular, authentic, hand crafted, family-recipe Thai dishes &#8211; without the soothing, sit-down Asian decor and award-winning wine list offered at Thai Sa-on.</p>
<p>But that isn’t to say it doesn’t have its own unique and attractive decor.</p>
<p>Featuring photos from the owner’s home land and a real Tuk Tuk crafted into a display case cooler, there are plenty attractions while you wait for your food.</p>
<p>Open late and providing a refreshing change from late-night burgers and pizza, Tuk Tuk Thai is the place to go for those who crave a little variety and aren’t afraid of a little spice!</p>
<div class='tm-tweet-clear'></div>
<div class='tm-click-to-tweet'>
<div class='tm-ctt-text'><a href='https://twitter.com/share?text=Tuk+Tuk+Thai+is+the+place+to+go+for+those+who+crave+a+little+variety&#038;via=calgaryregion&#038;related=calgaryregion&#038;url=http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/2016/02/10/5-hidden-culinary-treasures-calgary-region-inexpensive/' target='_blank'>Tuk Tuk Thai is the place to go for those who crave a little variety</a></div>

<div class='tm-ctt-tip'></div>
</div>
<p><strong><u>Top Five Dishes</u></strong></p>
<p><strong>Personal Favourite: </strong><br />
Moo Moo Lemon</p>
<p><strong>Authentic Dish: </strong><br />
Pad Thai with Chicken</p>
<p><strong>Veggie Lover: </strong><br />
Basa Garden</p>
<p><strong>Sweet Tooth: </strong><br />
Fried Bananas</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h2><strong>4. <a href="http://www.mlcafe.ca/" target="_blank">Evelyn&#8217;s Memory Lane Cafe</a></strong></h2>
<p><img class="alignright size-full wp-image-8538" src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/plugins/speed-booster-pack/inc/images/1x1.trans.gif" data-lazy-src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/CRP-Restaurants-300.jpg" alt="CRP Restaurants-300" width="300" height="200" /><noscript><img class="alignright size-full wp-image-8538" src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/CRP-Restaurants-300.jpg" alt="CRP Restaurants-300" width="300" height="200" /></noscript>It’s not always easy to write with any measure of certainty that a place can always be expected to consistently deliver deliciousness.</p>
<p>Especially one with a regularly changing menu, with features based on seasonal favourites</p>
<p>However, if you’ve ever been to High River’s Evelyn’ Memory Lane Cafe, you know this to be the case.</p>
<p>Just like the model train running around the roof and the mini jukeboxes in every booth &#8211; this longstanding cafe-style restaurant offers the type of fun, selection and comfort-style cooking you used to have at Grandma’s.</p>
<p>From shepherd&#8217;s pie to made to order sandwiches featuring Evelyn’s freshly made grain bread &#8211; it’s the type of place you always leave feeling good about what you ate.</p>
<div class='tm-tweet-clear'></div>
<div class='tm-click-to-tweet'>
<div class='tm-ctt-text'><a href='https://twitter.com/share?text=It%E2%80%99s+the+type+of+place+you+always+leave+feeling+good+about+what+you+ate.&#038;via=calgaryregion&#038;related=calgaryregion&#038;url=http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/2016/02/10/5-hidden-culinary-treasures-calgary-region-inexpensive/' target='_blank'>It’s the type of place you always leave feeling good about what you ate.</a></div>
<p><a href='https://twitter.com/share?text=It%E2%80%99s+the+type+of+place+you+always+leave+feeling+good+about+what+you+ate.&#038;via=calgaryregion&#038;related=calgaryregion&#038;url=http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/2016/02/10/5-hidden-culinary-treasures-calgary-region-inexpensive/' target='_blank' class='tm-ctt-btn'>Click To Tweet</a>
<div class='tm-ctt-tip'></div>
</div>
<p><img class="alignright size-full wp-image-8537" src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/plugins/speed-booster-pack/inc/images/1x1.trans.gif" data-lazy-src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/CRP-Restaurants-300-pie-crust.jpeg" alt="Calgary Region restaurants - pie crust" width="240" height="190" /><noscript><img class="alignright size-full wp-image-8537" src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/CRP-Restaurants-300-pie-crust.jpeg" alt="Calgary Region restaurants - pie crust" width="240" height="190" /></noscript></p>
<p>And don’t worry &#8211; just because it’s home style cooking, doesn’t mean you gluten-free, vegans and vegetarians don’t get their own tempting selections.</p>
<p>Not to mention the ever-rotating selections of homemade pies and even small-batch, handcrafted ice cream?</p>
<p>What can top that?</p>
<p><strong><u>Top Five Dishes</u></strong></p>
<p><strong>Personal Favourite:</strong><br />
Tough to say &#8211; is the chili on the menu, if not &#8211; Reuben Sandwich.</p>
<p><strong>Authentic Dish:</strong><br />
Fresh, handcrafted, small-batch ice cream.</p>
<p><strong>Veggie Lover: </strong><br />
Health Nut Sandwich</p>
<p><strong>Sweet Tooth:</strong><br />
Strawberry Rhubarb Pie</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h2><strong>5. <a href="http://www.dutchpancakes.ca/" target="_blank">Pfanntastic Pannenkoek Haus</a></strong></h2>
<p><img class="alignnone wp-image-8539 size-full" src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/plugins/speed-booster-pack/inc/images/1x1.trans.gif" data-lazy-src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/CRP-Restaurants-600-brithday.png" alt="Calgary Region restaurants - birthday" width="600" height="450" srcset="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/CRP-Restaurants-600-brithday-300x225.png 300w, http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/CRP-Restaurants-600-brithday-325x244.png 325w, http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/CRP-Restaurants-600-brithday-80x60.png 80w, http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/CRP-Restaurants-600-brithday.png 600w" sizes="(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px" /><noscript><img class="alignnone wp-image-8539 size-full" src="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/CRP-Restaurants-600-brithday.png" alt="Calgary Region restaurants - birthday" width="600" height="450" srcset="http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/CRP-Restaurants-600-brithday-300x225.png 300w, http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/CRP-Restaurants-600-brithday-325x244.png 325w, http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/CRP-Restaurants-600-brithday-80x60.png 80w, http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/CRP-Restaurants-600-brithday.png 600w" sizes="(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px" /></noscript></p>
<p>First thing &#8211; don’t show up here with a family of eight on Saturday morning and expect to be seated within the hour.</p>
<p>They are usually quite busy &#8211; and for a very good reason!</p>
<p>Yet, no matter how many times I talk about it socially, I keep meeting people who still haven’t had the pleasure.</p>
<p>Frankly, it doesn’t need my endorsement &#8211; and there isn’t much I can say about it that hasn’t already been covered by Global, the Food Network, You Gotta Eat Here! and a plethora of other reviews you can read on their walls.</p>
<p>Pfanntastic Pannenkoek Haus is a family-friendly, locally owned slice of authentic Holland cooking known worldwide for their Dutch &#8220;Pannenkoek&#8221; (similar to a crepe) served with toppings and fillings that are either savory or sweet.</p>
<p>It can be a meal or a treat. It’s the one place I’m willing to share my food with others. Well… willing to <em>trade</em>. It’s pretty fun to eat there.</p>
<p>Frankly, Pfanntastic Pannenkoek Haus, the only restaurant of its kind in Canada, is somewhere you need to experience to fully appreciate.</p>
<div class='tm-tweet-clear'></div>

<p><a href='https://twitter.com/share?text=The+only+restaurant+of+its+kind+in+Canada...somewhere+you+need+to+experience+to+fully+appreciate.&#038;via=calgaryregion&#038;related=calgaryregion&#038;url=http://www.calgaryregionfocus.com/2016/02/10/5-hidden-culinary-treasures-calgary-region-inexpensive/' target='_blank' class='tm-ctt-btn'>Click To Tweet</a>
<div class='tm-ctt-tip'></div>
</div>
<p><strong><u>Top Five Dishes</u></strong></p>
<p><strong>Personal Favourite: </strong><br />
Mushroom Soup (try it before your Pannenkoek)</p>
<p><strong>Savory Classic:</strong><br />
Potato, Onion, Bacon &amp; Cheese Pannenkoek (with a side of sour cream)</p>
<p><strong>Sweet Classic: </strong><br />
Banaan en chocoladesaus Pannenkoek (Banana and chocolate sauce)</p>
<p><strong>Have to Try: </strong><br />
Kaneel roll (Brown sugar, cinnamon, cream cheese icing and baked apple)</p>
<p><strong>__________</strong></p>
<p>There you have it &#8211; a 25-year insider’s review of restaurants you absolutely must try.</p>
<p><strong>Consider yourself deliciously informed!</strong></p>
<p><em>How about you? Do you have any favourite hidden local eats that you want to share?</em></p>
<p><em>Chad Hason</em><em> is a Canadian storyteller and owner of <a href="http://candidmar.com/" target="_blank">Candid MarCom</a>.</em></p>

						    	<div class="twinsbox" style="padding-bottom:0;">
		<h2>About the CRP</h2>		
		<span class="left bags2"></span>
		<p style="padding-bottom:30px;">The Calgary Regional Partnership (CRP) is a voluntary non-profit organization made up of twelve municipalities in the Calgary Region. Our Partnership protects the natural environment and watershed, fosters economic growth, develops a regional transportation network and plans growth for future generations.  The Calgary Region is home to approximately 1.2 million people and makes up 10,000 square kilometers of land and watershed.<br/>
		</p>
